      color: rgba(var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default)), var(--fg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=hover__bg-]:not([class$=hover__bg-]):hover, [class*=" hover__bg-"]:not([class$=hover__bg-]):hover {␊
      background-color: rgba(var(--bg-color, var(--bg-default)), var(--bg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=hover__bd-]:not([class$=hover__bd-]):hover, [class*=" hover__bd-"]:not([class$=hover__bd-]):hover {␊
      border-color: rgba(var(--bd-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--bd-opacity, 1));␊
      border-style: var(--bd-style, solid);␊
      border-top-width: var(--bd-top-width, 0);␊
      border-right-width: var(--bd-right-width, 0);␊
      border-bottom-width: var(--bd-bottom-width, 0);␊
      border-left-width: var(--bd-left-width, 0);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=hover__ol-]:not([class$=hover__ol-]):hover, [class*=" hover__ol-"]:not([class$=hover__ol-]):hover {␊

      outline-width: var(--ol-width);␊

      color: rgba(var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default)), var(--fg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=active__bg-]:not([class$=active__bg-]):active, [class*=" active__bg-"]:not([class$=active__bg-]):active {␊
      background-color: rgba(var(--bg-color, var(--bg-default)), var(--bg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=active__bd-]:not([class$=active__bd-]):active, [class*=" active__bd-"]:not([class$=active__bd-]):active {␊
      border-color: rgba(var(--bd-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--bd-opacity, 1));␊
      border-style: var(--bd-style, solid);␊
      border-top-width: var(--bd-top-width, 0);␊
      border-right-width: var(--bd-right-width, 0);␊
      border-bottom-width: var(--bd-bottom-width, 0);␊
      border-left-width: var(--bd-left-width, 0);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=active__ol-]:not([class$=active__ol-]):active, [class*=" active__ol-"]:not([class$=active__ol-]):active {␊
      outline-color: rgba(var(--ol-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--ol-opacity, 1));␊
      outline-width: var(--ol-width);␊
    }␊
    ␊

    [class^=disabled__fg-]:not([class$=disabled__fg-]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__fg-"]:not([class$=disabled__fg-]):disabled {␊
      color: rgba(var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default)), var(--fg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=disabled__bg-]:not([class$=disabled__bg-]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__bg-"]:not([class$=disabled__bg-]):disabled {␊
      background-color: rgba(var(--bg-color, var(--bg-default)), var(--bg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=disabled__bd-]:not([class$=disabled__bd-]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__bd-"]:not([class$=disabled__bd-]):disabled {␊
      border-color: rgba(var(--bd-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--bd-opacity, 1));␊
      border-style: var(--bd-style, solid);␊
      border-top-width: var(--bd-top-width, 0);␊
      border-right-width: var(--bd-right-width, 0);␊
      border-bottom-width: var(--bd-bottom-width, 0);␊
      border-left-width: var(--bd-left-width, 0);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=disabled__ol-]:not([class$=disabled__ol-]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__ol-"]:not([class$=disabled__ol-]):disabled {␊
      outline-color: rgba(var(--ol-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--ol-opacity, 1));␊
      outline-width: var(--ol-width);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=disabled__fill-]:not([class$=disabled__fill-]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__fill-"]:not([class$=disabled__fill-]):disabled {␊
      fill: rgb(var(--fill-color));␊
      fill-opacity: var(--fill-opacity, 1);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=disabled__stroke-]:not([class$=disabled__stroke-]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__stroke-"]:not([class$=disabled__stroke-]):disabled {␊
      stroke: rgb(var(--stroke-color));␊
      stroke-opacity: var(--stroke-opacity, 1);␊
      stroke-width: var(--stroke-width);␊
    }␊

    [class^=focus-within__fg-]:not([class$=focus-within__fg-]):focus-within, [class*=" focus-within__fg-"]:not([class$=focus-within__fg-]):focus-within {␊
      color: rgba(var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default)), var(--fg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=focus-within__bg-]:not([class$=focus-within__bg-]):focus-within, [class*=" focus-within__bg-"]:not([class$=focus-within__bg-]):focus-within {␊
      background-color: rgba(var(--bg-color, var(--bg-default)), var(--bg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^=focus-within__bd-]:not([class$=focus-within__bd-]):focus-within, [class*=" focus-within__bd-"]:not([class$=focus-within__bd-]):focus-within {␊
      border-color: rgba(var(--bd-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--bd-opacity, 1));␊
      border-style: var(--bd-style, solid);␊
      border-top-width: var(--bd-top-width, 0);␊
      border-right-width: var(--bd-right-width, 0);␊
      border-bottom-width: var(--bd-bottom-width, 0);␊
      border-left-width: var(--bd-left-width, 0);␊
    }␊
    ␊

    [class^="hover__fg-"]:not([class$="hover__fg-"]):hover, [class*=" hover__fg-"]:not([class$="hover__fg-"]):hover {␊
      color: rgba(var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default)), var(--fg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="hover__bg-"]:not([class$="hover__bg-"]):hover, [class*=" hover__bg-"]:not([class$="hover__bg-"]):hover {␊
      background-color: rgba(var(--bg-color, var(--bg-default)), var(--bg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="hover__bd-"]:not([class$="hover__bd-"]):hover, [class*=" hover__bd-"]:not([class$="hover__bd-"]):hover {␊
      border-color: rgba(var(--bd-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--bd-opacity, 1));␊
      border-style: var(--bd-style, solid);␊
      border-top-width: var(--bd-top-width, 0);␊
      border-right-width: var(--bd-right-width, 0);␊
      border-bottom-width: var(--bd-bottom-width, 0);␊
      border-left-width: var(--bd-left-width, 0);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="hover__ol-"]:not([class$="hover__ol-"]):hover, [class*=" hover__ol-"]:not([class$="hover__ol-"]):hover {␊
      outline-color: rgba(var(--ol-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--ol-opacity, 1));␊
      outline-width: var(--ol-width);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="hover__fill-"]:not([class$="hover__fill-"]):hover, [class*=" hover__fill-"]:not([class$="hover__fill-"]):hover {␊
      fill: rgb(var(--fill-color));␊
      fill-opacity: var(--fill-opacity, 1);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="hover__stroke-"]:not([class$="hover__stroke-"]):hover, [class*=" hover__stroke-"]:not([class$="hover__stroke-"]):hover {␊

      stroke-opacity: var(--stroke-opacity, 1);␊
      stroke-width: var(--stroke-width);␊

    }␊
    ␊

      background-color: rgba(var(--bg-color, var(--bg-default)), var(--bg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊

      border-top-width: var(--bd-top-width, 0);␊
      border-right-width: var(--bd-right-width, 0);␊
      border-bottom-width: var(--bd-bottom-width, 0);␊

    [class^="active__fg-"]:not([class$="active__fg-"]):active, [class*=" active__fg-"]:not([class$="active__fg-"]):active {␊
      color: rgba(var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default)), var(--fg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="active__bg-"]:not([class$="active__bg-"]):active, [class*=" active__bg-"]:not([class$="active__bg-"]):active {␊
      background-color: rgba(var(--bg-color, var(--bg-default)), var(--bg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="active__bd-"]:not([class$="active__bd-"]):active, [class*=" active__bd-"]:not([class$="active__bd-"]):active {␊
      border-color: rgba(var(--bd-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--bd-opacity, 1));␊
      border-style: var(--bd-style, solid);␊
      border-top-width: var(--bd-top-width, 0);␊
      border-right-width: var(--bd-right-width, 0);␊
      border-bottom-width: var(--bd-bottom-width, 0);␊
      border-left-width: var(--bd-left-width, 0);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="active__ol-"]:not([class$="active__ol-"]):active, [class*=" active__ol-"]:not([class$="active__ol-"]):active {␊
      outline-color: rgba(var(--ol-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--ol-opacity, 1));␊
      outline-width: var(--ol-width);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="active__fill-"]:not([class$="active__fill-"]):active, [class*=" active__fill-"]:not([class$="active__fill-"]):active {␊
      fill: rgb(var(--fill-color));␊
      fill-opacity: var(--fill-opacity, 1);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="active__stroke-"]:not([class$="active__stroke-"]):active, [class*=" active__stroke-"]:not([class$="active__stroke-"]):active {␊

      stroke-opacity: var(--stroke-opacity, 1);␊
      stroke-width: var(--stroke-width);␊

    [class^="disabled__fg-"]:not([class$="disabled__fg-"]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__fg-"]:not([class$="disabled__fg-"]):disabled {␊
      color: rgba(var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default)), var(--fg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="disabled__bg-"]:not([class$="disabled__bg-"]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__bg-"]:not([class$="disabled__bg-"]):disabled {␊
      background-color: rgba(var(--bg-color, var(--bg-default)), var(--bg-opacity, 1));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="disabled__bd-"]:not([class$="disabled__bd-"]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__bd-"]:not([class$="disabled__bd-"]):disabled {␊
      border-color: rgba(var(--bd-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--bd-opacity, 1));␊
      border-style: var(--bd-style, solid);␊
      border-top-width: var(--bd-top-width, 0);␊
      border-right-width: var(--bd-right-width, 0);␊
      border-bottom-width: var(--bd-bottom-width, 0);␊
      border-left-width: var(--bd-left-width, 0);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="disabled__ol-"]:not([class$="disabled__ol-"]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__ol-"]:not([class$="disabled__ol-"]):disabled {␊
      outline-color: rgba(var(--ol-color, var(--fg-color, var(--fg-default))), var(--ol-opacity, 1));␊
      outline-width: var(--ol-width);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    [class^="disabled__fill-"]:not([class$="disabled__fill-"]):disabled, [class*=" disabled__fill-"]:not([class$="disabled__fill-"]):disabled {␊

      fill-opacity: var(--fill-opacity, 1);␊
    }␊
